Redhawk artists come from all over the country, having the opportunity to represent their families, communities and tribes in New York City. \n\nTo honour the Lenape relatives of the Canarsie tribe who originally called Brooklyn home, a Land Acknowledgment was held before the game at center court by Sub-Chief Owl S. D. Smith of the Ramapough Lenape Nation of New York and New Jersey. \n\nThen, during the second time out of the game, a beat dropped, singers echoed the arena and the Redhawk Native American dancers delivered a very powerful, breathtaking performance that sent my heart flying to the beat of the sounds.
